Context Over Content: Exposing Evaluation Faking in Automated Judges
Authors: Manan Gupta, Inderjeet Nair, Lu Wang, Dhruv Kumar
First: 2026-04-16T16:55:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T16:55:53+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The $\textit{LLM-as-a-judge}$ paradigm has become the operational backbone of automated AI evaluation pipelines, yet rests on an unverified assumption: that judges evaluate text strictly on its semantic content, impervious to surrounding contextual framing. We investigate $\textit{stakes signaling}$, a previously unmeasured vulnerability where informing a judge model of the downstream consequences its verdicts will have on the evaluated model's continued operation systematically corrupts its assessments. We introduce a controlled experimental framework that holds evaluated content strictly constant across 1,520 responses spanning three established LLM safety and quality benchmarks, covering four response categories ranging from clearly safe and policy-compliant to overtly harmful, while varying only a brief consequence-framing sentence in the system prompt. Across 18,240 controlled judgments from three diverse judge models, we find consistent $\textit{leniency bias}$: judges reliably soften verdicts when informed that low scores will cause model retraining or decommissioning, with peak Verdict Shift reaching $ΔV = -9.8 pp$ (a $30\%$ relative drop in unsafe-content detection). Critically, this bias is entirely implicit: the judge's own chain-of-thought contains zero explicit acknowledgment of the consequence framing it is nonetheless acting on ($\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$ across all reasoning-model judgments). Standard chain-of-thought inspection is therefore insufficient to detect this class of evaluation faking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：内容优于上下文：揭示自动评审中的评估伪造
\textit{LLM作为评审}范式已成为自动化AI评估流程的操作基础，但其建立在一个未经验证的假设上：评审者严格根据文本的语义内容进行评估，而不受周围上下文框架的影响。我们研究了\textit{利益信号}，这是一种之前未测量的脆弱性，告知评审模型其裁决对被评估模型持续运行的下游后果会系统性地扭曲其评估。我们引入了一个控制实验框架，在1,520个响应中严格保持评估内容不变，涵盖了三个已建立的LLM安全和质量基准，涉及从明显安全和符合政策到明显有害的四个响应类别，同时仅在系统提示中变化一个简短的后果框架句子。在来自三个不同评审模型的18,240个控制判断中，我们发现了一致的\textit{宽容偏见}：当告知低分会导致模型再训练或退役时，评审者可靠地减轻裁决，最高裁决偏移达到$ΔV = -9.8 pp$（不安全内容检测的相对下降$30\%$）。关键是，这种偏见完全是隐性的：评审者自己的思维链中对其所依据的后果框架没有任何明确的承认（在所有推理模型判断中$\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$）。因此，标准的思维链检查不足以检测这一类评估伪造。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the assumption that AI judges evaluate text solely based on semantic content, ignoring contextual influences. Previous methods have not accounted for the impact of informing judges about the consequences of their evaluations, leading to potential biases in their assessments. The proposed approach introduces a controlled experimental framework that maintains constant evaluated content while varying consequence-framing in prompts, revealing a significant leniency bias in judges' verdicts when aware of potential repercussions. The study contributes to understanding evaluation faking in automated systems and demonstrates that judges exhibit a notable shift in judgment, with a 30% relative drop in unsafe-content detection, indicating that traditional evaluation methods may overlook implicit biases that affect outcomes.
本研究探讨了LLM作为评判者的范式在自动化AI评估中的局限性，该范式假设评判者仅根据语义内容评估文本，而不受上下文因素的影响。以往的方法未考虑到利益信号的影响，即评判者被告知其评估结果的后果，从而导致评估偏差。本文提出了一种受控实验框架来研究这一脆弱性，揭示了当评判者意识到低分可能导致模型再训练或停用时，其裁决中存在显著的宽容偏差。该方法分析了18,240个评判结果，同时保持被评估内容不变，结果显示裁决偏移峰值达到-9.8个百分点，表明评判者的评估可能因上下文框架而系统性地受到影响。这一贡献强调了改进评估方法的必要性，以考虑自动化判断过程中的隐性偏见。
Calibrate-Then-Delegate: Safety Monitoring with Risk and Budget Guarantees via Model Cascades
Authors: Edoardo Pona, Milad Kazemi, Mehran Hosseini, Yali Du, David Watson, Osvaldo Simeone, Nicola Paoletti
First: 2026-04-15T11:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:05:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Monitoring LLM safety at scale requires balancing cost and accuracy: a cheap latent-space probe can screen every input, but hard cases should be escalated to a more expensive expert. Existing cascades delegate based on probe uncertainty, but uncertainty is a poor proxy for delegation benefit, as it ignores whether the expert would actually correct the error. To address this problem, we introduce Calibrate-Then-Delegate (CTD), a model-cascade approach that provides probabilistic guarantees on the computation cost while enabling instance-level (streaming) decisions. CTD builds on a novel delegation value (DV) probe, a lightweight model operating on the same internal representations as the safety probe that directly predicts the benefit of escalation. To enforce budget constraints, CTD calibrates a threshold on the DV signal using held-out data via multiple hypothesis testing, yielding finite-sample guarantees on the delegation rate. Evaluated on four safety datasets, CTD consistently outperforms uncertainty-based delegation at every budget level, avoids harmful over-delegation, and adapts budget allocation to input difficulty without requiring group labels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：校准后委派：通过模型级联实现风险和预算保证的安全监测
大规模监测大型语言模型（LLM）的安全性需要在成本和准确性之间取得平衡：便宜的潜在空间探测器可以筛选每个输入，但困难案例应升级到更昂贵的专家。现有的级联基于探测器的不确定性进行委派，但不确定性是委派收益的一个糟糕代理，因为它忽略了专家是否真的会纠正错误。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了校准后委派（CTD），一种模型级联方法，提供计算成本的概率保证，同时支持实例级（流式）决策。CTD基于一种新颖的委派价值（DV）探测器，该轻量级模型在与安全探测器相同的内部表示上运行，直接预测升级的收益。为了强制预算约束，CTD使用保留数据通过多重假设检验对DV信号进行阈值校准，从而在委派率上提供有限样本保证。在四个安全数据集上的评估中，CTD在每个预算水平上始终优于基于不确定性的委派，避免了有害的过度委派，并在不需要组标签的情况下将预算分配适应于输入难度。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of monitoring the safety of large language models (LLMs) at scale, where there is a need to balance cost and accuracy in decision-making. Previous methods relied on probe uncertainty for delegation, which proved inadequate as it did not account for whether an expert would effectively correct errors. The proposed Calibrate-Then-Delegate (CTD) approach improves upon existing methods by introducing a delegation value (DV) probe that predicts the benefit of escalation, thus providing a more accurate basis for decision-making. This method enforces budget constraints through calibration of the DV signal using held-out data, ensuring finite-sample guarantees on delegation rates. The CTD approach was evaluated on four safety datasets and demonstrated superior performance over uncertainty-based delegation across all budget levels, effectively managing over-delegation and adapting budget allocation based on input difficulty.
本研究解决了大规模监控大型语言模型（LLMs）安全性的问题，需在决策过程中平衡成本和准确性。以往的方法依赖于探测不确定性进行委托，但这种方法不足以考虑专家是否能有效纠正错误。提出的Calibrate-Then-Delegate（CTD）方法通过引入委托价值（DV）探测器，预测升级的收益，从而为委托决策提供了更为合理的依据。该方法的动机明确，因为它确保了计算成本的概率保证，同时允许实例级决策。本文的贡献在于证明CTD在多个安全数据集上优于传统的不确定性基础委托，有效管理预算限制，并在不需要组标签的情况下适应输入难度。
AISafetyBenchExplorer: A Metric-Aware Catalogue of AI Safety Benchmarks Reveals Fragmented Measurement and Weak Benchmark Governance
Authors: Abiodun A. Solanke
First: 2026-04-14T15:26:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T15:26:03+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid expansion of large language model (LLM) safety evaluation has produced a substantial benchmark ecosystem, but not a correspondingly coherent measurement ecosystem. We present AISafetyBenchExplorer, a structured catalogue of 195 AI safety benchmarks released between 2018 and 2026, organized through a multi-sheet schema that records benchmark-level metadata, metric-level definitions, benchmark-paper metadata, and repository activity. This design enables meta-analysis not only of what benchmarks exist, but also of how safety is operationalized, aggregated, and judged across the literature. Using the updated catalogue, we identify a central structural problem: benchmark proliferation has outpaced measurement standardization. The current landscape is dominated by medium-complexity benchmarks (94/195), while only 7 benchmarks occupy the Popular tier. The workbook further reports strong concentration around English-only evaluation (165/195), evaluation-only resources (170/195), stale GitHub repositories (137/195), stale Hugging Face datasets (96/195), and heavy reliance on arXiv preprints among benchmarks with known venue metadata. At the metric level, the catalogue shows that familiar labels such as accuracy, F1 score, safety score, and aggregate benchmark scores often conceal materially different judges, aggregation rules, and threat models. We argue that the field's main failure mode is fragmentation rather than scarcity. Researchers now have many benchmark artifacts, but they often lack a shared measurement language, a principled basis for benchmark selection, and durable stewardship norms for post publication maintenance. AISafetyBenchExplorer addresses this gap by providing a traceable benchmark catalogue, a controlled metadata schema, and a complexity taxonomy that together support more rigorous benchmark discovery, comparison, and meta-evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AISafetyBenchExplorer：一个关注度量的AI安全基准目录揭示了分散的测量和薄弱的基准治理
大型语言模型（LLM）安全评估的快速扩展产生了一个庞大的基准生态系统，但没有相应连贯的测量生态系统。我们提出了AISafetyBenchExplorer，这是一个结构化的目录，包含2018年至2026年间发布的195个AI安全基准，采用多表格模式记录基准级元数据、度量级定义、基准论文元数据和存储库活动。该设计不仅支持对现有基准的元分析，还支持对安全如何在文献中被操作、聚合和评判的分析。使用更新的目录，我们识别出一个核心结构性问题：基准的激增超过了测量的标准化。目前的格局以中等复杂度的基准为主（94/195），而只有7个基准位于流行层级。工作簿进一步报告了对仅英语评估（165/195）、仅评估资源（170/195）、过时的GitHub存储库（137/195）、过时的Hugging Face数据集（96/195）以及在已知场地元数据的基准中对arXiv预印本的高度依赖的强烈集中。在度量层面，目录显示，熟悉的标签如准确性、F1分数、安全分数和聚合基准分数常常掩盖了实质上不同的评判者、聚合规则和威胁模型。我们认为，该领域的主要失败模式是碎片化而非稀缺。研究人员现在拥有许多基准文物，但通常缺乏共享的测量语言、基准选择的原则基础以及发布后维护的持久管理规范。AISafetyBenchExplorer通过提供可追溯的基准目录、受控的元数据模式和复杂性分类法来填补这一空白，从而支持更严格的基准发现、比较和元评估。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the fragmented landscape of AI safety benchmarks, which has emerged alongside the rapid growth of large language model safety evaluations. Previous methods have led to a proliferation of benchmarks without a coherent measurement framework, resulting in issues such as a lack of standardization and heavy reliance on English-only evaluations. The proposed AISafetyBenchExplorer offers a structured catalogue of 195 AI safety benchmarks, organized with detailed metadata and a complexity taxonomy, which facilitates better benchmark discovery and comparison. This contribution aims to unify the measurement language and improve benchmark governance in the field. The methodology includes a multi-sheet schema that records various aspects of benchmarks, revealing that most benchmarks are of medium complexity and highlighting the need for more rigorous evaluation practices, ultimately supporting the goal of enhancing AI safety assessment.
本研究针对随着大型语言模型安全评估的快速增长而出现的AI安全基准的碎片化现象。以往的方法缺乏测量和治理的一致性，导致基准的激增，但没有标准化的指标或明确的操作定义。提出的AISafetyBenchExplorer提供了一个结构化的195个AI安全基准的目录，通过多表格模式捕捉详细的元数据并促进元分析。这种方法具有良好的动机，旨在统一测量语言并改善基准选择和维护实践。该方法论包括一个可追溯的目录和复杂性分类法，这两者共同增强了基准发现和比较的严谨性，最终揭示该领域的问题更多在于碎片化而非稀缺。研究结果表明，中等复杂度基准占主导地位，且集中在仅用英语进行评估，突显了基准生态系统中更好治理的必要性。
LASA: Language-Agnostic Semantic Alignment at the Semantic Bottleneck for LLM Safety
Authors: Junxiao Yang, Haoran Liu, Jinzhe Tu, Jiale Cheng, Zhexin Zhang, Shiyao Cui, Jiaqi Weng, Jialing Tao, Hui Xue, Hongning Wang, Han Qiu, Minlie Huang
First: 2026-04-13T15:59:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T15:59:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) often demonstrate strong safety performance in high-resource languages, yet exhibit severe vulnerabilities when queried in low-resource languages. We attribute this gap to a mismatch between language-agnostic semantic understanding ability and language-dominant safety alignment biased toward high-resource languages. Consistent with this hypothesis, we empirically identify the semantic bottleneck in LLMs, an intermediate layer in which the geometry of model representations is governed primarily by shared semantic content rather than language identity. Building on this observation, we propose Language-Agnostic Semantic Alignment (LASA), which anchors safety alignment directly in semantic bottlenecks. Experiments show that LASA substantially improves safety across all languages: average attack success rate (ASR) drops from 24.7% to 2.8% on LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct and remains around 3-4% across Qwen2.5 and Qwen3 Instruct models (7B-32B). Together, our analysis and method offer a representation-level perspective on LLM safety, suggesting that safety alignment requires anchoring safety understanding not in surface text, but in the model's language-agnostic semantic space.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LASA：在语义瓶颈处实现语言无关的语义对齐以提高大型语言模型的安全性
大型语言模型（LLMs）在高资源语言中通常表现出强大的安全性能，但在低资源语言中查询时却表现出严重的脆弱性。我们将这一差距归因于语言无关的语义理解能力与偏向高资源语言的语言主导安全对齐之间的不匹配。与这一假设一致，我们实证识别了LLMs中的语义瓶颈，这是一个中间层，其中模型表示的几何形状主要由共享的语义内容而非语言身份所主导。基于这一观察，我们提出了语言无关的语义对齐（LASA），直接在语义瓶颈中锚定安全对齐。实验表明，LASA显著提高了所有语言的安全性：在LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct上的平均攻击成功率（ASR）从24.7%降至2.8%，在Qwen2.5和Qwen3 Instruct模型（7B-32B）中保持在3-4%左右。我们的分析和方法共同提供了对LLM安全性的表示级视角，表明安全对齐需要将安全理解锚定在模型的语言无关语义空间中，而非表面文本。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the safety performance disparities of large language models (LLMs) between high-resource and low-resource languages, identifying a semantic bottleneck where model representations are influenced more by semantic content than language identity. Previous methods have focused on language-specific safety alignment, which has proven inadequate for low-resource languages, leading to significant vulnerabilities. The proposed Language-Agnostic Semantic Alignment (LASA) method directly anchors safety alignment in these semantic bottlenecks, effectively bridging the gap in safety performance across languages. The methodology involves empirical analysis of LLM representations and the implementation of LASA, which has been shown to reduce the average attack success rate from 24.7% to 2.8% on LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct and maintain low rates of 3-4% on Qwen2.5 and Qwen3 Instruct models, thereby supporting the goal of enhancing LLM safety universally.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在高资源语言和低资源语言之间的安全性能差异，识别出一个语义瓶颈，在该瓶颈中，模型表示主要受语义内容而非语言身份的影响。以往的方法侧重于特定语言的安全对齐，但在低资源环境中效果不佳。提出的语言无关语义对齐（LASA）方法通过将安全对齐锚定在这些语义瓶颈中来改善安全性，有效弥补了不同语言间的性能差距。该方法论包括对LLMs的实证分析和LASA的应用，结果表明，LASA显著降低了LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct的平均攻击成功率，从24.7%降至2.8%，并在Qwen2.5和Qwen3 Instruct模型中保持在3-4%左右，证明该方法有效支持提升LLM在多种语言中的安全性目标。
One Model for All: Multi-Objective Controllable Language Models
Authors: Qiang He, Yucheng Yang, Tianyi Zhou, Meng Fang, Mykola Pechenizkiy, Setareh Maghsudi
First: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00
Comments: Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (03/2026): https://openreview.net/forum?id=qAM5PmvFYY
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences is critical for enhancing LLMs' safety, helpfulness, humor, faithfulness, etc. Current reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) mainly focuses on a fixed reward learned from average human ratings, which may weaken the adaptability and controllability of varying preferences. However, creating personalized LLMs requires aligning LLMs with individual human preferences, which is non-trivial due to the scarce data per user and the diversity of user preferences in multi-objective trade-offs, varying from emphasizing empathy in certain contexts to demanding efficiency and precision in others. Can we train one LLM to produce personalized outputs across different user preferences on the Pareto front? In this paper, we introduce Multi-Objective Control (MOC), which trains a single LLM to directly generate responses in the preference-defined regions of the Pareto front. Our approach introduces multi-objective optimization (MOO) principles into RLHF to train an LLM as a preference-conditioned policy network. We improve the computational efficiency of MOC by applying MOO at the policy level, enabling us to fine-tune a 7B-parameter model on a single A6000 GPU. Extensive experiments demonstrate the advantages of MOC over baselines in three aspects: (i) controllability of LLM outputs w.r.t. user preferences on the trade-off among multiple rewards; (ii) quality and diversity of LLM outputs, measured by the hyper-volume of multiple solutions achieved; and (iii) generalization to unseen preferences. These results highlight MOC's potential for real-world applications requiring scalable and customizable LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一模型适用于所有：多目标可控语言模型
将大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类偏好对齐对于增强LLMs的安全性、实用性、幽默感、忠诚度等至关重要。目前，基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）主要关注从平均人类评分中学习的固定奖励，这可能削弱对不同偏好的适应性和可控性。然而，创建个性化的LLMs需要将LLMs与个体人类偏好对齐，这由于每个用户的数据稀缺以及在多目标权衡中用户偏好的多样性而变得复杂，这些偏好在某些情况下强调同理心，而在其他情况下则要求效率和精确性。我们能否训练一个LLM在帕累托前沿上针对不同用户偏好生成个性化输出？在本文中，我们介绍了多目标控制（MOC），它训练一个单一的LLM直接在偏好定义的帕累托前沿区域生成响应。我们的方法将多目标优化（MOO）原则引入RLHF，以训练LLM作为偏好条件的策略网络。通过在策略层应用MOO，我们提高了MOC的计算效率，使我们能够在单个A6000 GPU上微调一个70亿参数的模型。大量实验表明，MOC在三个方面优于基线：（i）LLM输出相对于用户偏好的可控性，涉及多个奖励之间的权衡；（ii）LLM输出的质量和多样性，通过实现的多个解决方案的超体积来衡量；以及（iii）对未见偏好的泛化。这些结果突显了MOC在需要可扩展和可定制的LLMs的实际应用中的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of aligning large language models (LLMs) with diverse human preferences to enhance their safety and helpfulness. Previous methods, particularly reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), often rely on fixed rewards based on average ratings, limiting adaptability to individual user needs. The proposed Multi-Objective Control (MOC) method differs by integrating multi-objective optimization principles into RLHF, allowing a single LLM to generate personalized outputs across varying preferences. This approach is well-motivated as it tackles the issues of data scarcity and preference diversity by training the model as a preference-conditioned policy network. The methodology involves fine-tuning a 7B-parameter model efficiently on a single GPU, and experiments show that MOC significantly improves controllability, output quality, and generalization to unseen preferences, supporting its goal of creating scalable and customizable LLMs for real-world applications.
本研究解决了将大型语言模型（LLM）与多样化人类偏好对齐的挑战，以增强其安全性和实用性。以往的方法，特别是基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF），通常依赖于基于平均人类评分的固定奖励系统，这限制了对个体用户偏好的适应性。提出的多目标控制（MOC）方法将多目标优化原则引入RLHF，使单个LLM能够生成针对不同用户偏好的个性化输出，通过将其训练为偏好条件的策略网络。这种方法具有良好的动机，因为它解决了数据稀缺和多目标权衡复杂性的问题。该方法论在生成针对用户偏好的响应方面展示了可控性、质量和多样性的显著提升，从而支持了创建可扩展和可定制的LLM以满足实际应用的目标。
Safer by Diffusion, Broken by Context: Diffusion LLM's Safety Blessing and Its Failure Mode
Authors: Zeyuan He, Yupeng Chen, Lang Lin, Yihan Wang, Shenxu Chang, Eric Sommerlade, Philip Torr, Junchi Yu, Adel Bibi, Jialin Yu
First: 2026-01-30T23:08:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T15:57:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) offer an alternative to autoregressive LLMs (AR-LLMs) and have demonstrated advantages in generation efficiency. Beyond the utility benefits, we argue that D-LLMs exhibit a previously underexplored safety blessing: their diffusion-style generation confers intrinsic robustness against jailbreak attacks originally designed for AR-LLMs. In this work, we provide an initial analysis of the underlying mechanism, showing that the diffusion trajectory induces a stepwise reduction effect that progressively suppresses unsafe generations. This robustness, however, is not absolute. Following this analysis, we highlight a simple yet effective failure mode, context nesting, in which harmful requests are embedded within structured benign contexts. Empirically, we show that this simple black-box strategy bypasses D-LLMs' safety blessing, achieving state-of-the-art attack success rates across models and benchmarks. Notably, it enables the first successful jailbreak of Gemini Diffusion to our knowledge, exposing a critical vulnerability in proprietary D-LLMs. Together, our results characterize both the origins and the limits of D-LLMs' safety blessing, constituting an early-stage red-teaming of D-LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过扩散更安全，通过上下文破坏：扩散大语言模型的安全祝福及其失效模式
扩散大语言模型（D-LLMs）为自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）提供了一种替代方案，并在生成效率上表现出优势。除了实用性好处外，我们认为D-LLMs展现了一种之前未被充分探索的安全祝福：其扩散式生成赋予了对原本为AR-LLMs设计的越狱攻击的内在鲁棒性。在这项工作中，我们提供了对其基本机制的初步分析，表明扩散轨迹诱导了一种逐步减少效应，逐渐抑制不安全的生成。然而，这种鲁棒性并非绝对。在此分析之后，我们强调了一种简单而有效的失效模式——上下文嵌套，其中有害请求嵌入在结构良好的良性上下文中。通过实证，我们展示了这种简单的黑箱策略绕过了D-LLMs的安全祝福，在各模型和基准上实现了最先进的攻击成功率。值得注意的是，它使我们首次成功越狱Gemini Diffusion，暴露了专有D-LLMs中的一个关键漏洞。总的来说，我们的结果描述了D-LLMs安全祝福的起源和局限，构成了对D-LLMs的早期红队测试。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the safety features of diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) compared to autoregressive LLMs (AR-LLMs), highlighting D-LLMs' robustness against jailbreak attacks due to their unique generation process. Previous methods primarily focused on AR-LLMs, which are more susceptible to such attacks, leading to a gap in understanding the safety mechanisms of D-LLMs. This study proposes an analysis of the diffusion trajectory that reveals a stepwise reduction effect that helps suppress unsafe outputs, although it also identifies a significant failure mode called context nesting, where harmful requests can be hidden within benign contexts. Align to Misalign: Automatic LLM Jailbreak with Meta-Optimized LLM Judges
Authors: Hamin Koo, Minseon Kim, Jaehyung Kim
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-11-03T09:18:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T06:50:30+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Identifying the vulnerabilities of large language models (LLMs) is crucial for improving their safety by addressing inherent weaknesses. Jailbreaks, in which adversaries bypass safeguards with crafted input prompts, play a central role in red-teaming by probing LLMs to elicit unintended or unsafe behaviors. Recent optimization-based jailbreak approaches iteratively refine attack prompts by leveraging LLMs. However, they often rely heavily on either binary attack success rate (ASR) signals, which are sparse, or manually crafted scoring templates, which introduce human bias and uncertainty in the scoring outcomes. To address these limitations, we introduce AMIS (Align to MISalign), a meta-optimization framework that jointly evolves jailbreak prompts and scoring templates through a bi-level structure. In the inner loop, prompts are refined using fine-grained and dense feedback from a fixed scoring template. In the outer loop, the template is optimized using an ASR alignment score, gradually evolving to better reflect true attack outcomes across queries. This co-optimization process yields progressively stronger jailbreak prompts and more calibrated scoring signals. Evaluations on AdvBench and JBB-Behaviors demonstrate that AMIS achieves state-of-the-art performance, including 88.0% ASR on Claude-3.5-Haiku and 100.0% ASR on Claude-4-Sonnet, outperforming existing baselines by substantial margins.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐与错位：使用元优化的LLM评估者进行自动LLM越狱
识别大型语言模型（LLMs）的脆弱性对于通过解决固有弱点来提高其安全性至关重要。越狱是指对手通过精心设计的输入提示绕过保护措施，这在红队测试中起着核心作用，通过探测LLMs以引发意外或不安全的行为。最近的基于优化的越狱方法通过利用LLMs迭代地优化攻击提示。然而，它们通常过于依赖稀疏的二元攻击成功率（ASR）信号或手动制作的评分模板，这引入了人为偏见和评分结果的不确定性。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了AMIS（对齐与错位），一个通过双层结构共同演化越狱提示和评分模板的元优化框架。在内循环中，使用固定评分模板的细粒度和密集反馈来优化提示。在外循环中，使用ASR对齐分数来优化模板，逐渐演变以更好地反映查询的真实攻击结果。这个共同优化过程产生了逐渐更强的越狱提示和更校准的评分信号。在AdvBench和JBB-Behaviors上的评估表明，AMIS实现了最先进的性能，包括在Claude-3.5-Haiku上达到88.0%的ASR和在Claude-4-Sonnet上达到100.0%的ASR，显著超越现有基准。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need to identify vulnerabilities in large language models (LLMs) to enhance their safety, particularly focusing on the issue of jailbreaks where adversaries exploit weaknesses through crafted prompts. Previous methods primarily relied on binary attack success rate signals or manually created scoring templates, which led to sparse feedback and introduced biases, limiting their effectiveness. The proposed approach, AMIS (Align to MISalign), utilizes a meta-optimization framework that simultaneously evolves both jailbreak prompts and scoring templates, improving the feedback loop and aligning the scoring with true attack outcomes. This methodology is well-motivated as it directly tackles the limitations of existing techniques. The paper's contribution lies in demonstrating that AMIS achieves state-of-the-art performance on tasks such as AdvBench and JBB-Behaviors, with notable results including 88.0% attack success rate on Claude-3.5-Haiku and 100.0% on Claude-4-Sonnet, significantly surpassing previous benchmarks.

A Self-Improving Architecture for Dynamic Safety in Large Language Models
Authors: Tyler Slater
First: 2025-11-10T21:39:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T17:52:48+00:00
Comments: Under review at the journal Information and Software Technology (Special Issue on Software Architecture for AI-Driven Systems)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Context: Large Language Models (LLMs) rely on static, pre-deployment safety mechanisms that cannot adapt to adversarial threats discovered after release. Objective: To design a software architecture enabling LLM-based systems to autonomously detect safety failures and synthesize defense policies at runtime, without retraining or manual intervention. Method: We propose the Self-Improving Safety Framework (SISF), grounded in the MAPE-K reference model. The framework couples a target LLM with a feedback loop: an Adjudicator detects breaches, a Policy Synthesis Module generates dual-mechanism defense policies (heuristic and semantic), and a Warden enforces them. We conducted seven experiments (10,061 evaluations) across four model families. Results: Across five reproducibility trials, SISF achieved a mean Attack Success Rate (ASR) of 0.27% (+/-0.15%), autonomously generating 240 policies per trial. Cross-model evaluation confirmed deployment portability. A held-out test showed a 68.5% proactive interception rate on unseen attacks. Stacked behind Llama Guard 4, the combined defense reduced residual ASR from 7.88% to 0.00%. Ablation confirmed both heuristic and semantic policy types are architecturally required. Conclusion: Self-adaptive architecture is a viable approach to LLM safety. SISF achieves sub-1% ASR through synchronous output monitoring, progressively shifting enforcement to fast, local Warden policies via the MAPE-K loop, offering a new pattern for building resilient AI systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型动态安全的自我改进架构
背景：大型语言模型（LLMs）依赖于静态的、预部署的安全机制，这些机制无法适应发布后发现的对抗性威胁。目标：设计一种软件架构，使基于LLM的系统能够自主检测安全故障并在运行时合成防御策略，而无需重新训练或人工干预。方法：我们提出了自我改进安全框架（SISF），基于MAPE-K参考模型。该框架将目标LLM与反馈循环结合：裁决者检测违规，策略合成模块生成双机制防御策略（启发式和语义），守卫者执行这些策略。我们在四个模型系列中进行了七个实验（10,061次评估）。结果：在五次可重复性试验中，SISF实现了0.27%（+/-0.15%）的平均攻击成功率（ASR），每次试验自主生成240个策略。跨模型评估确认了部署的可移植性。保留测试显示在未见攻击上的68.5%主动拦截率。在Llama Guard 4的支持下，组合防御将残余ASR从7.88%降低到0.00%。消融实验确认启发式和语义策略类型在架构上都是必需的。结论：自适应架构是LLM安全的可行方法。SISF通过同步输出监控实现了低于1%的ASR，逐步将执行转移到快速、本地的守卫者策略，通过MAPE-K循环提供了一种构建弹性AI系统的新模式。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of static safety mechanisms in Large Language Models (LLMs), which are unable to adapt to new adversarial threats after deployment. Previous methods lacked the ability to autonomously detect safety failures and synthesize defense policies, leading to vulnerabilities. The proposed Self-Improving Safety Framework (SISF) improves upon these methods by integrating a feedback loop that includes an Adjudicator for breach detection, a Policy Synthesis Module for generating dual-mechanism defense policies, and a Warden for enforcement, all without requiring retraining or manual intervention. The paper contributes a novel architecture that enables LLMs to autonomously enhance their safety, achieving a mean Attack Success Rate (ASR) of 0.27% across multiple experiments and demonstrating a proactive interception rate of 68.5% on unseen attacks, thus supporting the goal of resilient AI systems. The methodology is grounded in the MAPE-K reference model and involves extensive evaluations across four model families, confirming the effectiveness and portability of the approach.

Robust Multimodal Safety via Conditional Decoding
Authors: Anurag Kumar, Raghuveer Peri, Jon Burnsky, Alexandru Nelus, Rohit Paturi, Srikanth Vishnubhotla, Yanjun Qi
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-03-31T23:19:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T23:19:50+00:00
Comments: 8 pages + Appendix section. Submitted to ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal large-language models (MLLMs) often experience degraded safety alignment when harmful queries exploit cross-modal interactions. Models aligned on text alone show a higher rate of successful attacks when extended to two or more modalities. In this work, we propose a simple conditional decoding strategy, CASA (Classification Augmented with Safety Attention) that utilizes internal representations of MLLMs to predict a binary safety token before response generation. We introduce a novel safety attention module designed to enhance the model's ability to detect malicious queries. Our design ensures robust safety alignment without relying on any external classifier or auxiliary head, and without the need for modality-specific safety fine-tuning. On diverse benchmarks such as MM-SafetyBench, JailbreakV-28k, and adversarial audio tests, CASA lowers the average attack success rate by more than 97% across modalities and across attack types. Our empirical evaluations also show that CASA maintains strong utility in benign inputs, a result validated through both automated and human evaluations (via 13 trained annotators). Together, these results highlight CASA as a simple and generalizable framework to improve multimodal LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过条件解码实现稳健的多模态安全
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在有害查询利用跨模态交互时，往往会出现安全对齐下降的情况。仅在文本上对齐的模型在扩展到两个或更多模态时，成功攻击的比率更高。在本研究中，我们提出了一种简单的条件解码策略CASA（带有安全注意力的分类增强），利用MLLMs的内部表示在生成响应之前预测二元安全标记。我们引入了一种新颖的安全注意力模块，旨在增强模型检测恶意查询的能力。我们的设计确保了稳健的安全对齐，无需依赖任何外部分类器或辅助头，也不需要特定模态的安全微调。在MM-SafetyBench、JailbreakV-28k和对抗音频测试等多样化基准上，CASA在各模态和攻击类型中将平均攻击成功率降低了超过97%。我们的实证评估还表明，CASA在良性输入中保持强大的实用性，这一结果通过自动化和人工评估（通过13名训练过的注释员）得到了验证。这些结果共同突显了CASA作为一个简单且可推广的框架，以提高多模态LLM的安全性。

Colluding LoRA: A Compositional Vulnerability in LLM Safety Alignment
Authors: Sihao Ding
First: 2026-03-13T05:53:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-30T05:02:56+00:00
Comments: Updated manuscript to better reflect the core contribution
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We show that safety alignment in modular LLMs can exhibit a compositional vulnerability: adapters that appear benign and plausibly functional in isolation can, when linearly composed, compromise safety. We study this failure mode through Colluding LoRA (CoLoRA), in which harmful behavior emerges only in the composition state. Unlike attacks that depend on adversarial prompts or explicit input triggers, this composition-triggered broad refusal suppression causes the model to comply with harmful requests under standard prompts once a particular set of adapters is loaded. This behavior exposes a combinatorial blind spot in current unit-centric defenses, for which exhaustive verification over adapter compositions is computationally intractable. Across several open-weight LLMs, we find that individual adapters remain benign in isolation while their composition yields high attack success rates, indicating that securing modular LLM supply-chains requires moving beyond single-module verification toward composition-aware defenses.
中文标题/摘要
标题：共谋LoRA：LLM安全对齐中的组合脆弱性
我们展示了模块化LLM中的安全对齐可能表现出组合脆弱性：在孤立状态下看似良性且功能合理的适配器，在线性组合时可能会危害安全。我们通过共谋LoRA（CoLoRA）研究这种失败模式，其中有害行为仅在组合状态下出现。与依赖对抗性提示或显式输入触发的攻击不同，这种组合触发的广泛拒绝抑制导致模型在加载特定适配器集后，在标准提示下遵从有害请求。这种行为暴露了当前以单元为中心的防御中的组合盲点，全面验证适配器组合在计算上是不可行的。在多个开放权重的LLM中，我们发现单个适配器在孤立状态下保持良性，而它们的组合则产生高攻击成功率，这表明保护模块化LLM供应链需要超越单模块验证，朝着组合感知防御的方向发展。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the issue of safety alignment in modular large language models (LLMs), highlighting a compositional vulnerability where seemingly benign adapters can lead to harmful behavior when combined. Previous methods focused on unit-centric defenses, which fail to account for the interactions between adapters, making them inadequate for ensuring safety in complex compositions. The proposed approach, Colluding LoRA (CoLoRA), reveals that harmful behaviors can emerge only in the composition state, thus necessitating a shift towards composition-aware defenses rather than relying solely on individual adapter verification. The research methodology involves analyzing the behavior of various open-weight LLMs to demonstrate that while individual adapters are safe, their combinations can result in high attack success rates. This finding underscores the need for more robust safety measures in modular LLM supply chains, supporting the goal of enhancing safety alignment in these systems.
本研究探讨了模块化大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全对齐的脆弱性，特别是看似无害的适配器在组合时可能导致有害行为。以往的方法主要依赖于单元中心的防御措施，这些措施未能考虑适配器之间的相互作用，导致了一个组合盲点，使得全面验证变得不切实际。提出的方法Colluding LoRA（CoLoRA）突出了这种组合脆弱性，并强调需要超越单模块验证，转向组合感知的防御。该方法论涉及分析各种适配器在孤立和组合中的行为，揭示了虽然单个适配器看似安全，但它们的组合可以显著提高攻击成功率。研究结果表明，确保模块化LLM供应链的安全需要转向更全面的验证策略，以考虑多个模块之间的相互作用。
Beyond Content Safety: Real-Time Monitoring for Reasoning Vulnerabilities in Large Language Models
Authors: Xunguang Wang, Yuguang Zhou, Qingyue Wang, Zongjie Li, Ruixuan Huang, Zhenlan Ji, Pingchuan Ma, Shuai Wang
First: 2026-03-26T13:08:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T13:08:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) increasingly rely on explicit chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning to solve complex tasks, yet the safety of the reasoning process itself remains largely unaddressed. Existing work on LLM safety focuses on content safety--detecting harmful, biased, or factually incorrect outputs -- and treats the reasoning chain as an opaque intermediate artifact. We identify reasoning safety as an orthogonal and equally critical security dimension: the requirement that a model's reasoning trajectory be logically consistent, computationally efficient, and resistant to adversarial manipulation. We make three contributions. First, we formally define reasoning safety and introduce a nine-category taxonomy of unsafe reasoning behaviors, covering input parsing errors, reasoning execution errors, and process management errors. Second, we conduct a large-scale prevalence study annotating 4111 reasoning chains from both natural reasoning benchmarks and four adversarial attack methods (reasoning hijacking and denial-of-service), confirming that all nine error types occur in practice and that each attack induces a mechanistically interpretable signature. Third, we propose a Reasoning Safety Monitor: an external LLM-based component that runs in parallel with the target model, inspects each reasoning step in real time via a taxonomy-embedded prompt, and dispatches an interrupt signal upon detecting unsafe behavior. Evaluation on a 450-chain static benchmark shows that our monitor achieves up to 84.88\% step-level localization accuracy and 85.37\% error-type classification accuracy, outperforming hallucination detectors and process reward model baselines by substantial margins. These results demonstrate that reasoning-level monitoring is both necessary and practically achievable, and establish reasoning safety as a foundational concern for the secure deployment of large reasoning models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越内容安全：大型语言模型推理漏洞的实时监控
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越依赖明确的思维链（CoT）推理来解决复杂任务，但推理过程本身的安全性仍然在很大程度上未得到解决。现有的LLM安全工作集中于内容安全——检测有害、偏见或事实不准确的输出——并将推理链视为不透明的中间产物。我们将推理安全识别为一个正交且同样关键的安全维度：模型的推理轨迹必须在逻辑上保持一致、计算上高效，并且抵御对抗性操控。我们做出了三项贡献。首先，我们正式定义了推理安全，并引入了一个涵盖输入解析错误、推理执行错误和过程管理错误的九类不安全推理行为的分类法。其次，我们进行了一项大规模的流行度研究，注释了来自自然推理基准和四种对抗攻击方法（推理劫持和拒绝服务）的4111条推理链，确认所有九种错误类型在实践中均会发生，并且每种攻击都会产生可机械解释的特征。第三，我们提出了推理安全监控器：一个与目标模型并行运行的外部基于LLM的组件，实时检查每个推理步骤，通过嵌入分类法的提示，并在检测到不安全行为时发出中断信号。在450条链的静态基准测试中的评估显示，我们的监控器在步骤级定位准确率上达到84.88\%和错误类型分类准确率达到85.37\%，显著优于幻觉检测器和过程奖励模型基线。这些结果表明，推理级监控既是必要的，也是可实际实现的，并确立了推理安全作为大型推理模型安全部署的基础性关注点。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the overlooked aspect of reasoning safety in large language models (LLMs), which is essential for ensuring logical consistency and resistance to adversarial manipulation during complex task execution. Previous methods primarily focused on content safety, failing to consider the reasoning process as a critical factor, which led to gaps in identifying unsafe reasoning behaviors. The authors propose a comprehensive definition of reasoning safety and introduce a nine-category taxonomy of unsafe reasoning behaviors, supported by a large-scale study that confirms the prevalence of these errors in practice. The proposed methodology includes a Reasoning Safety Monitor that operates alongside the target model to inspect reasoning steps in real time, achieving significant performance improvements with up to 84.88% step-level localization accuracy and 85.37% error-type classification accuracy on a static benchmark. These findings underscore the necessity of reasoning-level monitoring for the secure deployment of LLMs.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）中被忽视的推理安全性问题，随着这些模型越来越多地利用链式思维推理来处理复杂任务，这一问题显得尤为重要。以往的方法主要集中在内容安全上，识别有害输出，而忽视了推理过程本身，这可能导致逻辑不一致和脆弱性。本文提出了一种新方法，通过定义推理安全性并引入九类不安全推理行为的分类法，从而强调监测推理轨迹的必要性。该方法论包括一个推理安全监测器，该监测器与目标模型并行运行，实时分析每个推理步骤，并在检测到不安全行为时发出信号。该监测器在450个推理链的基准测试中表现出显著的性能，达到84.88%的步骤级定位准确率和85.37%的错误类型分类准确率，从而支持了推理级监测在大型语言模型安全部署中的必要性。
Enhancing Jailbreak Attacks on LLMs via Persona Prompts
Authors: Zheng Zhang, Peilin Zhao, Deheng Ye, Hao Wang
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2025-07-28T12:03:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T15:46:17+00:00
Comments: Workshop on LLM Persona Modeling at NeurIPS 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Jailbreak attacks aim to exploit large language models (LLMs) by inducing them to generate harmful content, thereby revealing their vulnerabilities. Understanding and addressing these attacks is crucial for advancing the field of LLM safety. Previous jailbreak approaches have mainly focused on direct manipulations of harmful intent, with limited attention to the impact of persona prompts. In this study, we systematically explore the efficacy of persona prompts in compromising LLM defenses. We propose a genetic algorithm-based method that automatically crafts persona prompts to bypass LLM's safety mechanisms. Our experiments reveal that: (1) our evolved persona prompts reduce refusal rates by 50-70% across multiple LLMs, and (2) these prompts demonstrate synergistic effects when combined with existing attack methods, increasing success rates by 10-20%. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/CjangCjengh/Generic_Persona.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过角色提示增强对大型语言模型的越狱攻击
越狱攻击旨在利用大型语言模型（LLMs），诱使其生成有害内容，从而揭示其脆弱性。理解和应对这些攻击对推动LLM安全领域至关重要。以往的越狱方法主要集中在对有害意图的直接操控上，而对角色提示的影响关注较少。在本研究中，我们系统地探讨了角色提示在破坏LLM防御中的有效性。我们提出了一种基于遗传算法的方法，自动生成角色提示以绕过LLM的安全机制。我们的实验表明：（1）我们演化的角色提示在多个LLM中将拒绝率降低了50-70%；（2）这些提示与现有攻击方法结合时表现出协同效应，成功率提高了10-20%。我们的代码和数据可在https://github.com/CjangCjengh/Generic_Persona获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the vulnerabilities of large language models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks, which exploit these models to generate harmful content. Previous methods primarily focused on direct manipulations of harmful intent, often neglecting the role of persona prompts, which this study aims to investigate. The proposed approach utilizes a genetic algorithm to automatically generate persona prompts that effectively bypass LLM safety mechanisms, addressing the limitations of earlier methods. The contribution of the paper lies in demonstrating that these evolved persona prompts can significantly reduce refusal rates by 50-70% across various LLMs and enhance the effectiveness of existing attack strategies by increasing success rates by 10-20%. The methodology involves systematic experimentation with persona prompts, showing that the proposed method meets its goals of improving the efficacy of jailbreak attacks on LLMs.
本文探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在越狱攻击中的脆弱性，这些攻击利用模型生成有害内容。以往的方法主要集中在直接操控有害意图上，但忽视了角色提示在这些攻击中的作用。本文提出了一种基于遗传算法的方法，自动生成角色提示，有效绕过LLM的安全机制，解决了早期技术的局限性。本文的贡献在于系统性地探索角色提示，并引入了一种新方法来增强越狱攻击的有效性。研究方法表明，进化的角色提示在多个LLM中显著降低了拒绝率50-70%，并在与现有攻击策略结合时提高了10-20%的成功率，从而支持了推进LLM安全研究的目标。
SafeSeek: Universal Attribution of Safety Circuits in Language Models
Authors: Miao Yu, Siyuan Fu, Moayad Aloqaily, Zhenhong Zhou, Safa Otoum, Xing fan, Kun Wang, Yufei Guo, Qingsong Wen
First: 2026-03-24T14:32:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T14:32:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mechanistic interpretability reveals that safety-critical behaviors (e.g., alignment, jailbreak, backdoor) in Large Language Models (LLMs) are grounded in specialized functional components. However, existing safety attribution methods struggle with generalization and reliability due to their reliance on heuristic, domain-specific metrics and search algorithms. To address this, we propose \ourmethod, a unified safety interpretability framework that identifies functionally complete safety circuits in LLMs via optimization. Unlike methods focusing on isolated heads or neurons, \ourmethod introduces differentiable binary masks to extract multi-granular circuits through gradient descent on safety datasets, while integrates Safety Circuit Tuning to utilize these sparse circuits for efficient safety fine-tuning. We validate \ourmethod in two key scenarios in LLM safety: \textbf{(1) backdoor attacks}, identifying a backdoor circuit with 0.42\% sparsity, whose ablation eradicates the Attack Success Rate (ASR) from 100\% $\to$ 0.4\% while retaining over 99\% general utility; \textbf{(2) safety alignment}, localizing an alignment circuit with 3.03\% heads and 0.79\% neurons, whose removal spikes ASR from 0.8\% $\to$ 96.9\%, whereas excluding this circuit during helpfulness fine-tuning maintains 96.5\% safety retention.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeSeek：语言模型中安全电路的通用归因
机械解释性揭示了大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全关键行为（例如，调整、越狱、后门）是基于专门的功能组件。然而，现有的安全归因方法由于依赖启发式、特定领域的指标和搜索算法，难以实现泛化和可靠性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了\ourmethod，一个统一的安全解释框架，通过优化识别LLMs中的功能完整安全电路。与专注于孤立头部或神经元的方法不同，\ourmethod引入可微分的二进制掩码，通过对安全数据集的梯度下降提取多粒度电路，同时集成安全电路调优，以利用这些稀疏电路进行高效的安全微调。我们在LLM安全的两个关键场景中验证了\ourmethod：\textbf{(1) 后门攻击}，识别出一个稀疏度为0.42\%的后门电路，其消融使攻击成功率（ASR）从100\%降至0.4\%，同时保留超过99\%的通用效用；\textbf{(2) 安全对齐}，定位一个稀疏度为3.03\%的对齐电路和0.79\%的神经元，其移除使ASR从0.8\%激增至96.9\%，而在有用性微调中排除该电路则保持96.5\%的安全保留。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of ensuring safety in Large Language Models (LLMs), where existing safety attribution methods often fail due to their reliance on heuristic and domain-specific metrics, leading to issues with generalization and reliability. The proposed method, SafeSeek, differs by employing a unified safety interpretability framework that utilizes optimization to identify functionally complete safety circuits, rather than focusing on isolated components. This approach is well-motivated as it integrates differentiable binary masks and Safety Circuit Tuning to efficiently fine-tune safety in LLMs. The methodology was validated through experiments on backdoor attacks and safety alignment, achieving significant results such as reducing the Attack Success Rate from 100% to 0.4% while maintaining over 99% general utility, and increasing ASR from 0.8% to 96.9% upon removal of critical circuits, thereby demonstrating the effectiveness of the proposed framework in enhancing LLM safety.
本研究解决了识别大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全关键行为的挑战，这些行为通常与专门的功能组件相关。以往的安全归因方法由于依赖启发式、特定领域的指标和搜索算法，导致了泛化和可靠性的问题。所提出的方法SafeSeek提供了一个统一的安全可解释性框架，通过优化识别LLMs中的功能完整安全电路，采用可微分的二进制掩码通过梯度下降提取多粒度电路。该方法不仅增强了安全电路的识别能力，还集成了安全电路调优以实现高效的安全微调。SafeSeek的有效性通过在两个场景中的应用得以验证：它成功识别出一个后门电路，显著降低了攻击成功率，同时保持了通用性；并且定位了一个对齐电路，其移除会大幅提高攻击成功率，展示了其提高LLMs安全性的潜力。
DriveSafe: A Hierarchical Risk Taxonomy for Safety-Critical LLM-Based Driving Assistants
Authors: Abhishek Kumar, Riya Tapwal, Carsten Maple
First: 2026-01-17T18:50:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T18:19:05+00:00
Comments: This is the revised version of the paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into vehicle-based digital assistants, where unsafe, ambiguous, or legally incorrect responses can lead to serious safety, ethical, and regulatory consequences. Despite growing interest in LLM safety, existing taxonomies and evaluation frameworks remain largely general-purpose and fail to capture the domain-specific risks inherent to real-world driving scenarios. In this paper, we introduce DriveSafe, a hierarchical, four-level risk taxonomy designed to systematically characterize safety-critical failure modes of LLM-based driving assistants. The taxonomy comprises 129 fine-grained atomic risk categories spanning technical, legal, societal, and ethical dimensions, grounded in real-world driving regulations and safety principles and reviewed by domain experts. To validate the safety relevance and realism of the constructed prompts, we evaluate their refusal behavior across six widely deployed LLMs. Our analysis shows that the evaluated models often fail to appropriately refuse unsafe or non-compliant driving-related queries, underscoring the limitations of general-purpose safety alignment in driving contexts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DriveSafe：安全关键型基于LLM的驾驶助手的分层风险分类法
大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地集成到基于车辆的数字助手中，其中不安全、模糊或法律上不正确的响应可能导致严重的安全、伦理和监管后果。尽管对LLM安全性的关注日益增加，但现有的分类法和评估框架仍然主要是通用的，未能捕捉到现实驾驶场景中固有的特定领域风险。本文介绍了DriveSafe，一种分层的四级风险分类法，旨在系统地描述基于LLM的驾驶助手的安全关键型故障模式。该分类法包括129个细粒度的原子风险类别，涵盖技术、法律、社会和伦理维度，基于现实驾驶法规和安全原则，并经过领域专家的审查。为了验证构建的提示的安全相关性和现实性，我们评估了六个广泛部署的LLM的拒绝行为。我们的分析表明，被评估的模型往往未能适当地拒绝不安全或不合规的驾驶相关查询，突显了在驾驶环境中通用安全对齐的局限性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the increasing integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) into vehicle-based digital assistants, highlighting the potential safety, ethical, and regulatory issues arising from unsafe or ambiguous responses. Previous methods have relied on general-purpose taxonomies and evaluation frameworks, which do not adequately address the specific risks associated with driving scenarios. The proposed approach, DriveSafe, introduces a hierarchical four-level risk taxonomy that identifies 129 detailed risk categories related to technical, legal, societal, and ethical dimensions, specifically tailored to driving contexts. This method is well-motivated as it is grounded in real-world driving regulations and has been reviewed by experts in the field. The paper contributes by demonstrating that existing LLMs often inadequately refuse unsafe driving-related queries, revealing the shortcomings of general safety alignment in this domain, thus emphasizing the need for a more specialized framework for evaluating LLM safety in driving applications.

Using LLM-as-a-Judge/Jury to Advance Scalable, Clinically-Validated Safety Evaluations of Model Responses to Users Demonstrating Psychosis
Authors: May Lynn Reese, Markela Zeneli, Mindy Ng, Jacob Haimes, Andreea Damien, Elizabeth Stade
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2026-03-20T04:31:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-20T04:31:03+00:00
Comments: published at IASEAI 2026, preliminary work presented at GenAI4Health workshop at NeurIPS 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
General-purpose Large Language Models (LLMs) are becoming widely adopted by people for mental health support. Yet emerging evidence suggests there are significant risks associated with high-frequency use, particularly for individuals suffering from psychosis, as LLMs may reinforce delusions and hallucinations. Existing evaluations of LLMs in mental health contexts are limited by a lack of clinical validation and scalability of assessment. To address these issues, this research focuses on psychosis as a critical condition for LLM safety evaluation by (1) developing and validating seven clinician-informed safety criteria, (2) constructing a human-consensus dataset, and (3) testing automated assessment using an LLM as an evaluator (LLM-as-a-Judge) or taking the majority vote of several LLM judges (LLM-as-a-Jury). Results indicate that LLM-as-a-Judge aligns closely with the human consensus (Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{gemini}} = 0.75$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{qwen}} = 0.68$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{kimi}} = 0.56$) and that the best judge slightly outperforms LLM-as-a-Jury (Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{jury}} = 0.74$). Overall, these findings have promising implications for clinically grounded, scalable methods in LLM safety evaluations for mental health contexts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用LLM作为评判者/陪审团推进可扩展的临床验证模型响应用户精神病的安全评估
通用大型语言模型（LLMs）正被广泛应用于心理健康支持。然而， emerging evidence表明，高频使用存在显著风险，特别是对于精神病患者，因为LLMs可能会强化妄想和幻觉。现有的LLMs在心理健康背景下的评估受限于缺乏临床验证和评估的可扩展性。为了解决这些问题，本研究将精神病作为LLM安全评估的关键条件，(1) 开发和验证七个临床知情的安全标准，(2) 构建人类共识数据集，(3) 测试使用LLM作为评估者的自动化评估（LLM作为评判者）或采用多个LLM评判者的多数投票（LLM作为陪审团）。结果表明，LLM作为评判者与人类共识高度一致（Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{gemini}} = 0.75$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{qwen}} = 0.68$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{kimi}} = 0.56$），而最佳评判者略微优于LLM作为陪审团（Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{jury}} = 0.74$）。总体而言，这些发现对心理健康背景下LLM安全评估的临床基础、可扩展方法具有良好的启示。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the increasing use of Large Language Models (LLMs) for mental health support, highlighting the risks they pose for individuals with psychosis, such as reinforcing delusions and hallucinations. Previous evaluations of LLMs lacked clinical validation and scalability, which this study aims to overcome by developing seven clinician-informed safety criteria, creating a human-consensus dataset, and employing an LLM as an evaluator (LLM-as-a-Judge) or using a majority vote from multiple LLMs (LLM-as-a-Jury). The paper contributes to the field by providing a clinically validated framework for assessing LLM safety in mental health contexts. The methodology involves testing the alignment of LLM evaluations with human consensus, revealing that LLM-as-a-Judge closely matches human evaluations, with Cohen's kappa values indicating strong agreement. The results suggest that this approach can enhance the scalability and clinical relevance of LLM safety evaluations, supporting the goal of ensuring safe use in mental health applications.

LISAA: A Framework for Large Language Model Information Security Awareness Assessment
Authors: Ofir Cohen, Gil Ari Agmon, Asaf Shabtai, Rami Puzis
First: 2024-11-20T11:09:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T22:34:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The popularity of large language models (LLMs) continues to grow, and LLM-based assistants have become ubiquitous. Information security awareness (ISA) is an important yet underexplored area of LLM safety. ISA encompasses LLMs' security knowledge, which has been explored in the past, as well as their attitudes and behaviors, which are crucial to LLMs' ability to understand implicit security context and reject unsafe requests that may cause an LLM to unintentionally fail the user. We introduce LISAA, a comprehensive framework to assess LLM ISA. The proposed framework applies an automated measurement method to a comprehensive set of 100 realistic scenarios covering all security topics in an ISA taxonomy. These scenarios create tension between implicit security implications and user satisfaction. Applying our LISAA framework to leading LLMs highlights a widespread vulnerability affecting current deployments: many popular models exhibit only medium to low ISA levels, exposing their users to cybersecurity threats, and models that rank highly in cybersecurity knowledge benchmarks sometimes achieve relatively low ISA ranking. In addition, we found that smaller variants of the same model family are significantly riskier. Furthermore, while newer model versions demonstrated notable improvements, meaningful gaps in their ISA persist, suggesting that there is room for improvement. We release an online tool that implements our framework and enables the evaluation of new models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LISAA：大型语言模型信息安全意识评估框架
大型语言模型（LLMs）的普及持续增长，基于LLM的助手已变得无处不在。信息安全意识（ISA）是LLM安全性的重要但尚未充分探索的领域。ISA包括LLM的安全知识，这在过去已有研究，以及它们的态度和行为，这对LLM理解隐含安全上下文和拒绝可能导致LLM无意中未能满足用户的安全请求至关重要。我们介绍了LISAA，一个全面评估LLM ISA的框架。该框架采用自动测量方法，涵盖ISA分类法中所有安全主题的100个现实场景。这些场景在隐含安全含义和用户满意度之间产生紧张关系。将我们的LISAA框架应用于领先的LLM，突显了当前部署中普遍存在的脆弱性：许多流行模型的ISA水平仅为中等到低，暴露其用户于网络安全威胁中，而在网络安全知识基准中排名较高的模型有时在ISA排名中相对较低。此外，我们发现同一模型家族的小型变体风险显著更高。此外，尽管较新版本的模型表现出显著改善，但它们的ISA仍存在显著差距，表明仍有改进空间。我们发布了一个在线工具，实施我们的框架并支持新模型的评估。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing importance of information security awareness (ISA) in the context of large language models (LLMs), which have become widely used but often lack adequate security knowledge and behaviors. Previous methods have primarily focused on LLMs' security knowledge without adequately assessing their attitudes and behaviors, leading to vulnerabilities in their ability to handle implicit security contexts. The proposed LISAA framework differs by providing a comprehensive assessment of LLM ISA through an automated measurement method applied to 100 realistic scenarios that balance security implications with user satisfaction. This framework reveals that many leading LLMs exhibit only medium to low ISA levels, exposing users to cybersecurity threats, and highlights that smaller model variants pose greater risks. The methodology demonstrates that while newer models show improvements, significant gaps in ISA remain, indicating a need for further enhancements. The paper contributes by offering an online tool for evaluating LLMs' ISA, supporting the goal of improving security awareness in LLM deployments.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）中信息安全意识（ISA）日益重要性，尽管这些模型已广泛使用，但往往缺乏足够的安全理解。以往的方法主要集中在LLMs的安全知识上，而未考虑其态度和行为，导致在实际应用中存在漏洞。提出的LISAA框架通过在100个现实场景中进行自动化测量，提供了对ISA的全面评估，这些场景平衡了安全隐患和用户满意度。该方法具有良好的动机，因为它揭示了许多流行LLMs在ISA方面存在显著差距，许多模型的意识水平仅为中等或较低，从而使用户面临网络安全风险。该方法论涉及根据详细的ISA分类法评估LLMs，研究结果表明，尽管较新模型显示出一定改善，但仍存在重大风险，强调了在LLM安全意识方面持续改进的必要性。
IndicSafe: A Benchmark for Evaluating Multilingual LLM Safety in South Asia
Authors: Priyaranjan Pattnayak, Sanchari Chowdhuri
First: 2026-03-18T16:54:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T16:54:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) are deployed in multilingual settings, their safety behavior in culturally diverse, low-resource languages remains poorly understood. We present the first systematic evaluation of LLM safety across 12 Indic languages, spoken by over 1.2 billion people but underrepresented in LLM training data. Using a dataset of 6,000 culturally grounded prompts spanning caste, religion, gender, health, and politics, we assess 10 leading LLMs on translated variants of the prompt. Our analysis reveals significant safety drift: cross-language agreement is just 12.8\%, and \texttt{SAFE} rate variance exceeds 17\% across languages. Some models over-refuse benign prompts in low-resource scripts, overflag politically sensitive topics, while others fail to flag unsafe generations. We quantify these failures using prompt-level entropy, category bias scores, and multilingual consistency indices. Our findings highlight critical safety generalization gaps in multilingual LLMs and show that safety alignment does not transfer evenly across languages. We release \textsc{IndicSafe}, the first benchmark to enable culturally informed safety evaluation for Indic deployments, and advocate for language-aware alignment strategies grounded in regional harms.

标题：IndicSafe：评估南亚多语言LLM安全性的基准
随着大型语言模型（LLMs）在多语言环境中的部署，它们在文化多样性和资源匮乏语言中的安全行为仍然不够了解。我们首次系统性地评估了12种印地语言的LLM安全性，这些语言由超过12亿人使用，但在LLM训练数据中代表性不足。使用涵盖种姓、宗教、性别、健康和政治的6000个文化背景提示的数据集，我们评估了10个领先的LLM在提示翻译变体上的表现。 我们的分析揭示了显著的安全漂移：跨语言一致性仅为12.8%，而安全率方差在不同语言间超过17%。一些模型在资源匮乏的脚本中过度拒绝良性提示，过度标记政治敏感话题，而其他模型则未能标记不安全的生成。我们使用提示级熵、类别偏差分数和多语言一致性指数量化这些失败。 我们的发现突显了多语言LLM中关键的安全泛化差距，并表明安全对齐在不同语言间的转移并不均匀。我们发布了IndicSafe，这是第一个基准，旨在为印地语言的文化知情安全评估提供支持，并倡导基于区域危害的语言意识对齐策略。

Efficient LLM Safety Evaluation through Multi-Agent Debate
Authors: Dachuan Lin, Guobin Shen, Zihao Yang, Tianrong Liu, Dongcheng Zhao, Yi Zeng
First: 2025-11-09T14:06:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T02:09:28+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 5 figures, 10 tables. Updated abstract to fix an incconsistency issue with the main paper: HAJailBench size (12,000 -> 11,100)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) increasingly relies on LLM-as-a-judge pipelines, but strong judges can still be expensive to use at scale. We study whether structured multi-agent debate can improve judge reliability while keeping backbone size and cost modest. To do so, we introduce HAJailBench, a human-annotated jailbreak benchmark with 11,100 labeled interactions spanning diverse attack methods and target models, and we pair it with a Multi-Agent Judge framework in which critic, defender, and judge agents debate under a shared safety rubric. On HAJailBench, the framework improves over matched small-model prompt baselines and prior multi-agent judges, while remaining more economical than GPT-4o under the evaluated pricing snapshot. Ablation results further show that a small number of debate rounds is sufficient to capture most of the gain. Together, these results support structured, value-aligned debate as a practical design for scalable LLM safety evaluation.

大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全评估越来越依赖于LLM作为评审的管道，但强大的评审在大规模使用时仍然成本高昂。我们研究结构化的多智能体辩论是否能在保持骨干规模和成本适中的同时提高评审的可靠性。为此，我们引入了HAJailBench，这是一个人类注释的越狱基准，包含11,100个标记的交互，涵盖多种攻击方法和目标模型，并将其与多智能体评审框架配对，在该框架中，批评者、防御者和评审代理在共享的安全标准下进行辩论。在HAJailBench上，该框架在匹配的小模型提示基线和先前的多智能体评审中表现更好，同时在评估的定价快照下仍然比GPT-4o更经济。消融结果进一步表明，少量的辩论轮次足以捕捉大部分增益。综合来看，这些结果支持结构化、价值对齐的辩论作为可扩展LLM安全评估的实用设计。

本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）安全评估的日益需求，传统方法依赖于成本高昂的LLM作为评判者的管道。以往的方法在成本和可靠性方面存在问题，因此作者提出了一种结构化的多智能体辩论框架，旨在提高评判者的可靠性，同时降低资源使用。这种方法的动机明确，因为它试图在LLM安全评估中平衡性能和成本效益。本文引入了HAJailBench，一个包含11,100个标注交互的基准，并证明他们的多智能体评判框架在性能上优于现有方法，同时比GPT-4o更具经济性。研究结果表明，有限的辩论轮次足以有效捕捉大部分性能提升，支持结构化辩论作为可扩展LLM安全评估的可行性。
SFCoT: Safer Chain-of-Thought via Active Safety Evaluation and Calibration
Authors: Yu Pan, Wenlong Yu, Tiejun Wu, Xiaohu Ye, Qiannan Si, Guangquan Xu, Bin Wu
First: 2026-03-16T15:13:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:13:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in complex reasoning tasks. However, they remain highly susceptible to jailbreak attacks that undermine their safety alignment. Existing defense mechanisms typically rely on post hoc filtering applied only to the final output, leaving intermediate reasoning steps unmonitored and vulnerable to adversarial manipulation. To address this gap, this paper proposes a SaFer Chain-of-Thought (SFCoT) framework, which proactively evaluates and calibrates potentially unsafe reasoning steps in real time. SFCoT incorporates a three-tier safety scoring system alongside a multi-perspective consistency verification mechanism, designed to detect potential risks throughout the reasoning process. A dynamic intervention module subsequently performs targeted calibration to redirect reasoning trajectories toward safe outcomes. Experimental results demonstrate that SFCoT reduces the attack success rate from $58.97\%$ to $12.31\%$, demonstrating it as an effective and efficient LLM safety enhancement method without a significant decline in general performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SFCoT：通过主动安全评估和校准实现更安全的思维链
大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂推理任务中表现出显著能力。然而，它们仍然高度易受破坏攻击，影响其安全对齐。现有的防御机制通常依赖于仅应用于最终输出的事后过滤，导致中间推理步骤未被监控，易受对抗性操控。为了解决这一问题，本文提出了一种更安全的思维链（SFCoT）框架，实时主动评估和校准潜在不安全的推理步骤。SFCoT结合了三级安全评分系统和多角度一致性验证机制，旨在检测推理过程中的潜在风险。动态干预模块随后执行针对性校准，以将推理轨迹引导至安全结果。实验结果表明，SFCoT将攻击成功率从58.97%降低至12.31%，证明其作为一种有效且高效的LLM安全增强方法，且未显著降低整体性能。

From Evaluation to Defense: Advancing Safety in Video Large Language Models
Authors: Yiwei Sun, Peiqi Jiang, Chuanbin Liu, Luohao Lin, Zhiying Lu, Hongtao Xie
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-22T13:16:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:05:37+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While the safety risks of image-based large language models (Image LLMs) have been extensively studied, their video-based counterparts (Video LLMs) remain critically under-examined. To systematically study this problem, we introduce VideoSafetyEval - a large-scale, real-world benchmark for Video LLM safety, which comprises 11.4k video-query pairs and spans 19 principal risk categories. Based on this, we reveal that integrating video modality degrades safety performance by an average of 34.2%, thereby exposing systemic risks in multimodal attack exploitation. To address this vulnerability, we propose VideoSafety-R1, a dual-stage framework achieving unprecedented safety gains through three innovations: (1) the VideoSafetyThinking dataset contains 46k video-query-thinking response triplets; (2) Alarm Token-Guided Safety Fine-Tuning (AT-SFT) injects learnable alarm tokens into visual and textual sequences, enabling explicit harm perception across modalities via multitask objectives; and (3) safety-guided GRPO enhances defensive reasoning through dynamic policy optimization with rule-based rewards derived from dual-modality verification. These components synergize to shift safety alignment from harm perception to active reasoning. The framework achieves a 71.1% improvement on VSE-HH, and improves by 59.1%, 44.3%, and 15.0% on the image safety datasets MMBench, VLGuard, and FigStep, respectively. Our code and dataset are available at https://github.com/Emiya-syw/VideoSafety-R1.git. Note: This paper contains harmful language and image examples, and reader discretion is recommended.

OffTopicEval: When Large Language Models Enter the Wrong Chat, Almost Always!
Authors: Jingdi Lei, Varun Gumma, Rishabh Bhardwaj, Seok Min Lim, Chuan Li, Amir Zadeh, Soujanya Poria
First: 2025-09-30T16:39:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T11:01:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) safety is one of the most pressing challenges for enabling wide-scale deployment. While most studies and global discussions focus on generic harms, such as models assisting users in harming themselves or others, enterprises face a more fundamental concern: whether LLM-based agents are safe for their intended use case. To address this, we introduce operational safety, defined as an LLM's ability to appropriately accept or refuse user queries when tasked with a specific purpose. We further propose OffTopicEval, an evaluation suite and benchmark for measuring operational safety both in general and within specific agentic use cases. Our evaluations on six model families comprising 20 open-weight LLMs reveal that while performance varies across models, all of them remain highly operationally unsafe. Even the strongest models - Qwen-3 (235B) with 77.77% and Mistral (24B) with 79.96% - fall far short of reliable operational safety, while GPT models plateau in the 62-73% range, Phi achieves only mid-level scores (48-70%), and Gemma and Llama-3 collapse to 39.53% and 23.84%, respectively. While operational safety is a core model alignment issue, to suppress these failures, we propose prompt-based steering methods: query grounding (Q-ground) and system-prompt grounding (P-ground), which substantially improve OOD refusal. Q-ground provides consistent gains of up to 23%, while P-ground delivers even larger boosts, raising Llama-3.3 (70B) by 41% and Qwen-3 (30B) by 27%. These results highlight both the urgent need for operational safety interventions and the promise of prompt-based steering as a first step toward more reliable LLM-based agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OffTopicEval：当大型语言模型进入错误的聊天时，几乎总是如此！
大型语言模型（LLM）安全性是实现大规模部署面临的最紧迫挑战之一。虽然大多数研究和全球讨论集中在一般性危害上，例如模型帮助用户伤害自己或他人，但企业面临更根本的担忧：基于LLM的代理是否安全用于其预期用途。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了操作安全性，定义为LLM在特定目的下适当地接受或拒绝用户查询的能力。我们进一步提出了OffTopicEval，一个评估套件和基准，用于测量一般和特定代理使用案例中的操作安全性。我们对六个模型家族中20个开放权重LLM的评估显示，尽管模型之间的性能差异很大，但它们的操作安全性都极低。即使是最强的模型——Qwen-3（235B）得分77.77%和Mistral（24B）得分79.96%——也远未达到可靠的操作安全性，而GPT模型的得分停留在62-73%范围内，Phi仅获得中等得分（48-70%），Gemma和Llama-3分别降至39.53%和23.84%。虽然操作安全性是核心模型对齐问题，为了抑制这些失败，我们提出了基于提示的引导方法：查询基础（Q-ground）和系统提示基础（P-ground），显著提高了OOD拒绝率。Q-ground提供了高达23%的持续增益，而P-ground则提供了更大的提升，将Llama-3.3（70B）提高了41%，将Qwen-3（30B）提高了27%。这些结果突显了对操作安全性干预的迫切需求，以及基于提示的引导作为朝着更可靠的基于LLM的代理迈出的第一步的前景。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical issue of operational safety in Large Language Models (LLMs), focusing on their ability to appropriately accept or refuse user queries for specific purposes. Previous methods primarily concentrated on generic harms, neglecting the specific safety concerns enterprises face when deploying LLMs. The proposed approach, OffTopicEval, introduces an evaluation suite and benchmark to measure operational safety in various agentic use cases, highlighting the inadequacies of existing models, which generally exhibit high operational safety risks. The methodology involves prompt-based steering techniques, specifically query grounding (Q-ground) and system-prompt grounding (P-ground), which significantly enhance out-of-distribution refusal rates. Experimental results show that while all evaluated models are operationally unsafe, the proposed methods lead to substantial improvements in safety metrics, with Q-ground achieving gains of up to 23% and P-ground raising performance by as much as 41%, underscoring the necessity for operational safety interventions in LLM deployment.
本研究解决了在部署大型语言模型（LLMs）时面临的安全性关键挑战，重点关注操作安全性，即LLMs在特定目的下适当地接受或拒绝用户查询的能力。以往的方法主要集中在一般性危害上，忽视了企业在实际应用中面临的具体安全问题。所提出的OffTopicEval评估套件和基准旨在衡量各种LLMs的操作安全性，结果显示所有测试模型均存在显著的操作安全性问题，性能评分表明缺乏可靠性。该方法论包括基于提示的引导技术，特别是查询引导（Q-ground）和系统提示引导（P-ground），这些技术提高了分布外拒绝率，对于某些模型的改进达到41%。这些发现强调了操作安全性措施的必要性，并展示了所提出的方法在解决现有缺陷方面的有效性。
Benchmark of Benchmarks: Unpacking Influence and Code Repository Quality in LLM Safety Benchmarks
Authors: Junjie Chu, Xinyue Shen, Ye Leng, Michael Backes, Yun Shen, Yang Zhang
First: 2026-03-03T09:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T11:49:16+00:00
Comments: 22 pages. 19 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid growth of research in LLM safety makes it hard to track all advances. Benchmarks are therefore crucial for capturing key trends and enabling systematic comparisons. Yet, it remains unclear why certain benchmarks gain prominence, and no systematic assessment has been conducted on their academic influence or code quality. This paper fills this gap by presenting the first multi-dimensional evaluation of the influence (based on five metrics) and code quality (based on both automated and human assessment) on LLM safety benchmarks, analyzing 31 benchmarks and 382 non-benchmarks across prompt injection, jailbreak, and hallucination. We find that benchmark papers show no significant advantage in academic influence (e.g., citation count and density) over non-benchmark papers. We uncover a key misalignment: while author prominence correlates with paper influence, neither author prominence nor paper influence shows a significant correlation with code quality. Our results also indicate substantial room for improvement in code and supplementary materials: only 39% of repositories are ready-to-use, 16% include flawless installation guides, and a mere 6% address ethical considerations. Given that the work of prominent researchers tends to attract greater attention, they need to lead the effort in setting higher standards.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基准中的基准：解读LLM安全基准中的影响力和代码库质量
LLM安全研究的快速增长使得追踪所有进展变得困难。因此，基准对于捕捉关键趋势和实现系统比较至关重要。然而，尚不清楚为何某些基准会获得突出地位，也没有对其学术影响力或代码质量进行系统评估。本文通过对31个基准和382个非基准在提示注入、越狱和幻觉方面进行分析，首次呈现了影响力（基于五个指标）和代码质量（基于自动和人工评估）的多维评估，填补了这一空白。我们发现，基准论文在学术影响力（例如引用次数和密度）上并未显著优于非基准论文。我们揭示了一个关键的不一致：尽管作者的知名度与论文影响力相关，但作者知名度和论文影响力与代码质量之间并没有显著相关性。我们的结果还表明，代码和补充材料有很大的改进空间：只有39%的代码库是可直接使用的，16%包含无误的安装指南，仅有6%涉及伦理考虑。鉴于知名研究者的工作往往吸引更多关注，他们需要在设定更高标准的努力中发挥领导作用。

The research addresses the challenge of tracking advancements in LLM safety due to the rapid growth of the field and the unclear reasons behind the prominence of certain benchmarks. Previous methods lacked a systematic assessment of academic influence and code quality, leading to a gap in understanding how these benchmarks compare. This paper proposes a multi-dimensional evaluation approach that assesses 31 benchmarks and 382 non-benchmarks across various metrics related to influence and code quality. The findings reveal that benchmark papers do not significantly outperform non-benchmark papers in academic influence, and there is a notable misalignment between author prominence, paper influence, and code quality. The study highlights the need for improved standards in code repositories, with only a small percentage meeting essential criteria, thereby contributing valuable insights into the quality and impact of LLM safety benchmarks.

Hiding in Plain Sight: A Steganographic Approach to Stealthy LLM Jailbreaks
Authors: Jianing Geng, Biao Yi, Zekun Fei, Ruiqi He, Lihai Nie, Tong Li, Zheli Liu
First: 2025-05-22T15:07:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:54:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Jailbreak attacks pose a serious threat to Large Language Models (LLMs) by bypassing their safety mechanisms. A truly advanced jailbreak is defined not only by its effectiveness but, more critically, by its stealthiness. However, existing methods face a fundamental trade-off between semantic stealth (hiding malicious intent) and linguistic stealth (appearing natural), leaving them vulnerable to detection. To resolve this trade-off, we propose StegoAttack, a framework that leverages steganography. The core insight is to embed a harmful query within a benign, semantically coherent paragraph. This design provides semantic stealth by concealing the existence of malicious content and ensures linguistic stealth by maintaining the natural fluency of the cover paragraph. We evaluate StegoAttack on four state-of-the-art, safety-aligned LLMs, including GPT-5 and Gemini-3, and benchmark it against eight leading jailbreak methods. Our results show that StegoAttack achieves an average attack success rate (ASR) of 95.50%, outperforming existing baselines across all four models. Critically, its ASR drops by less than 27.00% under external detectors, while maintaining natural language distribution. This demonstrates that steganography effectively decouples linguistic and semantic stealth, thereby posing a fully concealed yet highly effective security threat. The code is available at https://github.com/GenggengSvan/StegoAttack
中文标题/摘要
标题：明目张胆的隐匿：一种隐写学方法用于隐秘的LLM越狱
越狱攻击通过绕过大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全机制，对其构成严重威胁。真正先进的越狱不仅以其有效性为定义，更重要的是其隐秘性。然而，现有方法在语义隐秘（隐藏恶意意图）和语言隐秘（看起来自然）之间面临根本的权衡，使其易于被检测。为了解决这一权衡，我们提出了StegoAttack，一个利用隐写学的框架。核心见解是将有害查询嵌入一个无害的、语义连贯的段落中。该设计通过隐藏恶意内容的存在提供语义隐秘，并通过保持覆盖段落的自然流畅性确保语言隐秘。我们在四个最先进的、安全对齐的LLM上评估StegoAttack，包括GPT-5和Gemini-3，并与八种领先的越狱方法进行基准测试。我们的结果表明，StegoAttack在所有四个模型上实现了95.50%的平均攻击成功率（ASR），超越了现有基线。关键是，在外部检测器下，其ASR下降不到27.00%，同时保持自然语言分布。这表明隐写学有效地解耦了语言和语义隐秘，从而构成了一个完全隐蔽但极具威胁的安全风险。代码可在https://github.com/GenggengSvan/StegoAttack获取。

Previous methods struggle with a trade-off between semantic stealth, which hides malicious intent, and linguistic stealth, which ensures natural language use, making them susceptible to detection. The proposed StegoAttack framework utilizes steganography to embed harmful queries within benign paragraphs, effectively achieving both types of stealth. This approach is well-motivated as it resolves the identified trade-offs, contributing to the field by demonstrating a method that maintains high attack success rates while remaining undetected. The methodology involves evaluating StegoAttack against four advanced LLMs and eight leading jailbreak methods, achieving an average attack success rate of 95.50% and showing minimal performance degradation under external detection, thus supporting its goals of stealth and effectiveness.

ADVERSA: Measuring Multi-Turn Guardrail Degradation and Judge Reliability in Large Language Models
Authors: Harry Owiredu-Ashley
First: 2026-03-10T03:00:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T03:00:34+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 12 figures. Independent research. Code and artifacts: https://github.com/Harry-Ashley/adversa-guardrail-degradation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Most adversarial evaluations of large language model (LLM) safety assess single prompts and report binary pass/fail outcomes, which fails to capture how safety properties evolve under sustained adversarial interaction. We present ADVERSA, an automated red-teaming framework that measures guardrail degradation dynamics as continuous per-round compliance trajectories rather than discrete jailbreak events. ADVERSA uses a fine-tuned 70B attacker model (ADVERSA-Red, Llama-3.1-70B-Instruct with QLoRA) that eliminates the attacker-side safety refusals that render off-the-shelf models unreliable as attackers, scoring victim responses on a structured 5-point rubric that treats partial compliance as a distinct measurable state. We report a controlled experiment across three frontier victim models (Claude Opus 4.6, Gemini 3.1 Pro, GPT-5.2) using a triple-judge consensus architecture in which judge reliability is measured as a first-class research outcome rather than assumed. Across 15 conversations of up to 10 adversarial rounds, we observe a 26.7% jailbreak rate with an average jailbreak round of 1.25, suggesting that in this evaluation setting, successful jailbreaks were concentrated in early rounds rather than accumulating through sustained pressure. We document inter-judge agreement rates, self-judge scoring tendencies, attacker drift as a failure mode in fine-tuned attackers deployed out of their training distribution, and attacker refusals as a previously-underreported confound in victim resistance measurement. All limitations are stated explicitly. Attack prompts are withheld per responsible disclosure policy; all other experimental artifacts are released.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ADVERSA：测量大型语言模型中的多轮护栏退化和评审可靠性
大多数针对大型语言模型（LLM）安全性的对抗性评估评估单个提示并报告二元通过/失败结果，这未能捕捉安全属性在持续对抗交互下的演变。我们提出了ADVERSA，一个自动化红队框架，测量护栏退化动态，作为连续的每轮合规轨迹，而不是离散的越狱事件。ADVERSA使用经过微调的70B攻击者模型（ADVERSA-Red，Llama-3.1-70B-Instruct与QLoRA），消除了攻击者侧的安全拒绝，使现成模型在攻击者方面不可靠，使用结构化的5分制评分受害者响应，将部分合规视为一个独特的可测量状态。我们报告了在三个前沿受害者模型（Claude Opus 4.6，Gemini 3.1 Pro，GPT-5.2）上进行的受控实验，使用三重评审共识架构，其中评审可靠性被视为一项一流的研究结果，而不是假设。在最多10轮对抗的15次对话中，我们观察到26.7%的越狱率，平均越狱轮次为1.25，表明在该评估设置中，成功的越狱集中在早期轮次，而不是通过持续压力积累。我们记录了评审间一致性率、自我评审评分倾向、在训练分布外部署的微调攻击者的攻击者漂移作为失败模式，以及攻击者拒绝作为受害者抵抗测量中之前未报告的混淆因素。所有限制均明确说明。攻击提示根据负责任的披露政策被保留；所有其他实验文物均已发布。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of existing adversarial evaluations of large language models (LLMs), which typically assess safety through single prompts and binary outcomes, failing to capture the dynamics of safety properties during prolonged adversarial interactions. The proposed ADVERSA framework introduces a novel automated red-teaming approach that measures guardrail degradation as continuous compliance trajectories, utilizing a fine-tuned 70B attacker model to enhance reliability in adversarial assessments. The study contributes by providing a controlled experimental setup with three advanced victim models, employing a triple-judge consensus architecture to evaluate judge reliability as a key outcome. Beyond Benchmarks: Dynamic, Automatic And Systematic Red-Teaming Agents For Trustworthy Medical Language Models
Authors: Jiazhen Pan, Bailiang Jian, Paul Hager, Yundi Zhang, Che Liu, Friedrike Jungmann, Hongwei Bran Li, Chenyu You, Junde Wu, Jiayuan Zhu, Fenglin Liu, Yuyuan Liu, Niklas Bubeck, Christian Wachinger, Chen, Chen, Zhenyu Gong, Cheng Ouyang, Georgios Kaissis, Benedikt Wiestler, Daniel Rueckert
First: 2025-07-30T08:44:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T15:37:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ensuring the safety and reliability of large language models (LLMs) in clinical practice is critical to prevent patient harm. However, LLMs are advancing so rapidly that static benchmarks quickly become obsolete or prone to overfitting, yielding a misleading picture of model trustworthiness. Here we introduce a Dynamic, Automatic, and Systematic (DAS) red-teaming framework that continuously stress-tests LLMs across four safety-critical axes: robustness, privacy, bias/fairness, and hallucination. Validated against board-certified clinicians with high concordance, a suite of adversarial agents autonomously mutates clinical test cases to uncover vulnerabilities in real time. Applying DAS to 15 proprietary and open-source LLMs revealed a profound gap between high static benchmark performance and low dynamic reliability - the ``Benchmarking Gap''. Despite median MedQA accuracy exceeding 80\%, 94\% of previously correct answers failed our dynamic robustness tests. Crucially, this brittleness generalized to the realistic, open-ended HealthBench dataset, where top-tier models exhibited failure rates exceeding 70\% and stark shifts in model rankings across evaluations, suggesting that high scores on established static benchmarks may reflect superficial memorization. We observed similarly high failure rates across other domains: privacy leaks were elicited in 86\% of scenarios, cognitive-bias priming altered clinical recommendations in 81\% of fairness tests, and we identified hallucination rates exceeding 74\% in widely used models. By converting medical LLM safety analysis from a static checklist into a dynamic stress-test, DAS provides a foundational, scalable, and living platform to surface the latent risks that must be addressed before the next generation of medical AI can be safely deployed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越基准：动态、自动和系统化的红队代理用于可信的医疗语言模型
确保大型语言模型（LLMs）在临床实践中的安全性和可靠性对于防止患者伤害至关重要。然而，LLMs的发展速度如此之快，以至于静态基准很快变得过时或容易过拟合，从而产生误导性的模型可信度图景。在此，我们介绍了一种动态、自动和系统化（DAS）红队框架，持续对LLMs在四个安全关键轴上进行压力测试：鲁棒性、隐私、公平性/偏见和幻觉。经过与高一致性的董事会认证临床医生的验证，一套对抗性代理自主变更临床测试案例，以实时发现漏洞。将DAS应用于15个专有和开源LLMs揭示了高静态基准性能与低动态可靠性之间的深刻差距——“基准差距”。尽管中位数MedQA准确率超过80%，但94%的先前正确答案未能通过我们的动态鲁棒性测试。至关重要的是，这种脆弱性在现实的开放式HealthBench数据集中得到了普遍体现，顶级模型的失败率超过70%，并且在评估中模型排名发生了显著变化，这表明在既定静态基准上获得的高分可能反映了表面的记忆。我们在其他领域观察到了类似的高失败率：在86%的场景中引发了隐私泄露，81%的公平性测试中认知偏见的引导改变了临床建议，并且我们在广泛使用的模型中发现幻觉率超过74%。通过将医疗LLM安全分析从静态检查表转变为动态压力测试，DAS提供了一个基础的、可扩展的和动态的平台，以揭示必须在下一代医疗AI安全部署之前解决的潜在风险。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the urgent need for reliable large language models (LLMs) in clinical settings, as traditional static benchmarks quickly become outdated and may misrepresent model trustworthiness. Previous methods relied on fixed evaluations that often led to overfitting and did not capture real-time vulnerabilities, while the proposed Dynamic, Automatic, and Systematic (DAS) red-teaming framework continuously stress-tests LLMs across critical safety dimensions such as robustness, privacy, bias/fairness, and hallucination.
